25:T4dc,You who believe, when you contract a debt for a stated term, put it down in writing: have a scribe write it down justly between you. No scribe should refuse to write: let him write as God has taught him, let the debtor dictate, and let him fear God, his Lord, and not diminish &#91;the debt&#93; at all. If the debtor is feeble-minded, weak, or unable to dictate, then let his guardian dictate justly. Call in two men as witnesses. If two men are not there, then call one man and two women out of those you approve as witnesses, so that if one of the two women should forget the other can remind her. Let the witnesses not refuse when they are summoned. Do not disdain to write the debt down, be it small or large, along with the time it falls due: this way is more equitable in God&rsquo;s eyes, more reliable as testimony, and more likely to prevent doubts arising between you. But if the merchandise is there and you hand it over, there is no blame on you if you do not write it down. Have witnesses present whenever you trade with one another, and let no harm be done to either scribe or witness, for if you did cause them harm, it would be a crime on your part. Be mindful of God, and He will teach you: He has full knowledge of everything26:T697,<entryFree id="n372" key="أخّر" type="main">

                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> The <hi rend="ital">back, hinder,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">latter, part:</hi> the <hi rend="ital">hindermost,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">last, part: contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">قُدُمٌ</foreign>. (K.) [See also <foreign lang="ar">مُؤَخَّرٌ</foreign>; from which it appears to be distinguished by its being used only adverbially, or with a preposition: and see <foreign lang="ar">آخِرٌ</foreign>.] You say, <foreign lang="ar">شُقَّ ثَوْبُهُ أُخُرًا</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">مِنْ أُخُرٍ</foreign>, (S, K, *) <hi rend="ital">His garment was rent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">slit, in its back,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">hinder, part,</hi> (S,) or <hi rend="ital">behind.</hi> (K.) And <foreign lang="ar">تَأَخَّرَ أُخُرًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He retired backwards</hi>]. (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">جَآءِ أُخُرًا</foreign>: see <foreign lang="ar">آخِرٌ</foreign>, in two places.    </entryFree>2a:T1761,<entryFree id="n386" key="آخَرُ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">آخَرُ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">آخر</orth>
                  </form> a subst., of the measure <foreign lang="ar">أَفْعَلُ</foreign>, but implying the meaning of an epithet, (S,) from <foreign lang="ar">أَخَّرَ</foreign> in the sense of <foreign lang="ar">تَأَخَّرَ</foreign>, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">Another;</hi> the <hi rend="ital">other; a thing</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">person</hi>] <hi rend="ital">other than the former</hi> or <hi rend="ital">first;</hi> (L;) <hi rend="ital">i. q.</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">غَيْرٌ</foreign>; (K;) as in the phrases, <foreign lang="ar">رَجُلٌ آخَرُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">another man,</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">ثَوْبٌ آخَرُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">another garment</hi> or <hi rend="ital">piece of cloth:</hi> (TA:) or <hi rend="ital">one of two things</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">persons</hi>]; (S, Sgh, Msb;) as when you say, <foreign lang="ar">جَآءَ القَوْمُ فَوَاحِدٌ يَفْعَلُ كَذَا وَآخَرُ كَذَا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The people came, and one was doing thus, and one</hi> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">another] thus:</hi> (Sgh, Msb:) originally meaning <hi rend="ital">more backward:</hi> (TA:) fem.   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n386-1" target="أُخْرَى" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> (S, Msb, K) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n386-2" target="أُخْرَاةٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n380"/></foreign>; (K) which latter is not well known: (MF:) pl. masc. <foreign lang="ar">آخَرُونَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أُخَرُ</foreign>; (S, K;) [the latter irreg. as such;] and, applied to irrational things, <foreign lang="ar">أَوَاخِرُ</foreign>, like as <foreign lang="ar">أَفَاضِلُ</foreign> is pl. of <foreign lang="ar">أَفْضَلُ</foreign>: (Msb:) and pl. fem. <foreign lang="ar">إُخْرَيَاتٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">إُخَرُ</foreign>; (S, Msb, K;) which latter is imperfectly decl.; for an epithet of the measure <foreign lang="ar">أَفْعَلُ</foreign> which is accompanied by <foreign lang="ar">مِنْ</foreign> has no [dual nor] pl. nor fem. as long as it is indeterminate; but when it has the article <foreign lang="ar">ال</foreign> prefixed to it, or is itself prefixed to another noun which it governs in the gen. case, it has a dual and a pl. and a fem.; but it is not so with <foreign lang="ar">آخَرُ</foreign>; for it has a fem. [and dual] and pl. without <foreign lang="ar">مِنْ</foreign> and without the article <foreign lang="ar">ال</foreign> and without its being prefixed to another noun: you say, <foreign lang="ar">مَرَرْتُ بِرَخُلٍ آخَرَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">بِرِجَالٍ أُخَرَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">آخَرِينَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">بِاٌمْرَأَةٍ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">بِنِسْوَةٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I passed by another man,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">by other men,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">by another woman,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">by other women;</hi>] therefore, as it [namely <foreign lang="ar">إُخَرُ</foreign>] is thus made to deviate from its original form, [i. e. <foreign lang="ar">آخَرُ</foreign>, (I' Ak p. 287,) which is of a class of words used, when indeterminate, alike as sing. and dual and pl.,] and is [essentially and originally] an epithet, it is imperfectly decl., <pb n="32"/> though a pl.: but when you name thereby a man, it is perfectly decl., when inderminate, accord. to Akh, or imperfectly decl. accord. to Sb. (S, L.) The dim. of <foreign lang="ar">آخَرُ</foreign> is   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n386-3" target="أُوَيْخِرُ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n389"/></foreign>; the <foreign lang="ar">ا</foreign> with the <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign> suppressed following the same rule as the <foreign lang="ar">ا</foreign> in <foreign lang="ar">ضَارِبٌ</foreign>: (TA:) and the dim. of <foreign lang="ar">إُخْرَى</foreign> is   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n386-4" target="أُخَيْرَى" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n385"/></foreign>. (S.) See also <foreign lang="ar">الأُخْرَى</foreign> voce <foreign lang="ar">آخِرٌ</foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">لَا أَفْعَلُهُ أُخْرَى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">اللَّيَالِى</foreign>, (S, K,) or <foreign lang="ar">اخرى المَنُونِ</foreign>, (K,) means <hi rend="ital">I will not do it ever:</hi> (S, K:) or the latter, <hi rend="ital">I will not do it to the end of time.</hi> (S.) And <foreign lang="ar">أُخْرَى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">القَوْمِ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">The last of the people.</hi> (S, K.) One says, <foreign lang="ar">جَآءَ فِى أُخْرَى القَوْمِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He came among the last of the people.</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">جَآءِ فِى أُخْرَيَاتِ النَّاسِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He came among those who were the last of the people.</hi> (S, A, K.) [See also <foreign lang="ar">آخِرٌ</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  In <foreign lang="ar">أَبْعَدَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">اللّٰهُ الآخَرَ</foreign>, the last word is a mistake for <foreign lang="ar">الأَخِرَ</foreign> q. v. (Meshárik of 'Iyád.)    </entryFree>2b:T305f,<entryFree id="n387" key="آخِرٌ" type="main">

                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">مُؤْخِرُ العَيْنِ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (T, S, A, Mgh, Msb, K, [in the CK <foreign lang="ar">مُؤَخَّرها</foreign>,]) said by AO, (Msb,) or A 'Obeyd, (TA,) to be better without teshdeed, from which observation it is to be understood that teshdeed in this case is allowable, though rare, but Az disallows it, (Msb, TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">مُؤْخِرَتُهَا</foreign>, and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n390-1" target="آخِرَتُهَا" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (K,) [<hi rend="ital">The outer angle of the eye;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">the part of the eye next the temple;</hi> (S, A, Mgh, Msb;) <hi rend="ital">the part next the</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">لَحَاظ</foreign>: (K:) opposed to its <foreign lang="ar">مُقْدِم</foreign>, which is the extremity thereof next the nose: (S, Mgh, Msb:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">مَآخِرُ</foreign>. (Mgh.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">إَلَيَّ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بِمُؤْخِرِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He looked at,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">towards, me from</hi> (lit. <hi rend="ital">with</hi>) <hi rend="ital">the outer angle of his eye</hi>]. (S.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">مُؤْخِرُ الرَّحْلِ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">مُؤْخِرَتُهُ</foreign>: see <foreign lang="ar">آخِرٌ</foreign>.
